
        --====================================== 1 ASSET CUMA BISA PUNYA 1 MAIN DOC
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  '1 ASSET CUMA BISA PUNYA 1 MAIN DOC' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DOC.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT COUNT(IS_MAIN_DOC) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET_ID
                    FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC WITH(NOLOCK)
                    GROUP BY ASSET_ID
                    HAVING COUNT(IS_MAIN_DOC) > 1
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET DOC CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI REF ASSET DOC
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET DOC CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI REF ASSET DOC' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT 
                    AD.ASSET_DOC_CODE, COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_ASSET_DOC RAD WITH(NOLOCK) ON RAD.ASSET_DOC_CODE = AD.ASSET_DOC_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE RAD.REF_ASSET_DOC_ID IS NULL 
                   GROUP BY AD.ASSET_DOC_CODE
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET DOC HARUS TERDAPAT PADA TIPE ASSET YANG VALID
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET DOC HARUS TERDAPAT PADA TIPE ASSET YANG VALID' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT AD.ASSET_DOC_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET A WITH(NOLOCK) ON A.ASSET_ID = AD.ASSET_ID
                   LEFT JOIN dbo.ASSET_TYPE AT WITH(NOLOCK) ON AT.ASSET_TYPE_CODE = A.ASSET_TYPE_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   LEFT JOIN dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST ADL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ADL.R2_ASSET_TYPE_ID = AT.R2_ASSET_TYPE_ID
                   WHERE ADL.ASSET_DOC_LIST_ID IS NULL
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== BRC LOCATION OFFICE CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI REF OFFICE
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'BRC LOCATION OFFICE CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI REF OFFICE' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.BRC_LOCATION_OFFICE_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.BRC_LOCATION_OFFICE_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT 
                    AD.BRC_LOCATION_OFFICE_CODE, COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_OFFICE RO WITH(NOLOCK) ON AD.BRC_LOCATION_OFFICE_CODE = RO.OFFICE_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE RO.REF_OFFICE_ID IS NULL
                   GROUP BY AD.BRC_LOCATION_OFFICE_CODE
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== FILING CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI FILING
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'FILING CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI FILING' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.FILING_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.FILING_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, AD.FILING_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.FILING F WITH(NOLOCK) ON F.FILING_CODE = AD.FILING_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE F.FILING_ID IS NULL
                   GROUP BY AD.FILING_CODE
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== JIKA DOC STAT CODE BRW, BRW DT DAN EXPECTED RETURN DT HARUS DIISI
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'JIKA DOC STAT CODE BRW, BRW DT DAN EXPECTED RETURN DT HARUS DIISI' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.DOC_NO' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.DOC_NO AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT AD.DOC_NO
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE AD.DOC_STAT_CODE = 'BRW' AND ( AD.BRW_DT IS NULL OR AD.EXPECTED_RETURN_DT IS NULL)
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== JIKA DOC STAT CODE ITR, IN PROCESSS STAT CODE ITR
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'JIKA DOC STAT CODE ITR, IN PROCESSS STAT CODE ITR' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT AD.ASSET_DOC_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE AD.DOC_STAT_CODE = 'ITR' AND AD.IN_PROCESS_STAT_CODE != 'ITR'
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ITR DESTOFFICE CODE JIKA ADA ISI, HARUS KEDAFTAR DI REF OFFICE
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ITR DESTOFFICE CODE JIKA ADA ISI, HARUS KEDAFTAR DI REF OFFICE' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, AD.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_OFFICE RF WITH(NOLOCK) ON RF.OFFICE_CODE = AD.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE RF.REF_OFFICE_ID IS NULL AND AD.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE IS NOT NULL
                   GROUP BY AD.ITR_DEST_OFFICE_CODE
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCESSORY CODE HARUS KEDAFTAR DI ASSET_ACCESSORY FOUNDATION
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ACCESSORY CODE HARUS KEDAFTAR DI ASSET_ACCESSORY FOUNDATION' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, AC.ACCESSORY_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY AC WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.ASSET_ACCESSORY AAC WITH(NOLOCK) ON AAC.ASSET_ACCESSORY_CODE = AC.ACCESSORY_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE AAC.ASSET_ACCESSORY_ID IS NULL
                   GROUP BY AC.ACCESSORY_CODE
                ) AS ACCESSORY
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SUPPL CODE HARUS KEDAFTAR DI VENDOR FOUNDATION YANG TYPE NY SUPPLIER
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SUPPL CODE HARUS KEDAFTAR DI VENDOR FOUNDATION YANG TYPE NY SUPPLIER' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ACCESSORY.SUPPL_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ACCESSORY.SUPPL_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT A.SUPPL_CODE, COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.VENDOR V WITH(NOLOCK) ON A.SUPPL_CODE = V.VENDOR_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AND V.MR_VENDOR_CATEGORY_CODE = 'SUPPLIER' COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE V.VENDOR_ID IS NULL
                   GROUP BY A.SUPPL_CODE
                ) AS ACCESSORY
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCESSORY PRICE AMT HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ACCESSORY PRICE AMT HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT a.ACCESSORY_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE A.ACCESSORY_PRICE_AMT <= 0
                ) AS ACCESSORY
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCESSORY RECEIVE DATE TIDAK BOLEH NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK

            )

                   SELECT  A.ACCESSORY_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY_OPL A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE a.ACCESSORY_RECEIVE_DT IS NULL
                ) AS ACCESSORY_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCESSORY OPL BASE TAX AMT & VAT AMT HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,

            )
            Select  'ACCESSORY OPL BASE TAX AMT & VAT AMT HARUS > 0' ,

                SELECT 'ACCESSORY_OPL.ACCESSORY_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ACCESSORY_OPL.ACCESSORY_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT  A.ACCESSORY_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY_OPL A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE A.BASE_TAX_AMT <= 0 AND A.VAT_AMT <= 0
                ) AS ACCESSORY_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SEMUA ACCESSORY HARUS PUNYA ACCESSORY OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SEMUA ACCESSORY HARUS PUNYA ACCESSORY OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ACCESSORY.ACCESSORY_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT A.ACCESSORY_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT OUTER JOIN AMS.dbo.ACCESSORY_OPL AOPL WITH(NOLOCK) ON AOPL.ACCESSORY_ID = A.ACCESSORY_ID
                   WHERE AOPL.ACCESSORY_OPL_ID IS NULL
                ) AS ACCESSORY
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== CUST OFFICE PERLU ADA DI FOU
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'CUST OFFICE PERLU ADA DI FOU' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.OFFICE_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.OFFICE_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, AAM.OFFICE_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING AAM WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_OFFICE RO WITH(NOLOCK) ON AAM.OFFICE_CODE = RO.OFFICE_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE RO.OFFICE_CODE IS NULL
                   GROUP BY AAM.OFFICE_CODE
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== AGRMNT PERLU ADA DI LMS
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'AGRMNT PERLU ADA DI LMS' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO' AS [TABLE] ,
                AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, AAM.AGRMNT_NO
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING AAM WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN LMS.dbo.AGRMNT AGR WITH(NOLOCK) ON AAM.AGRMNT_NO = AGR.AGRMNT_NO COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI
                   WHERE AGR.AGRMNT_NO IS NULL
                   GROUP BY AAM.AGRMNT_NO
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== 1 AGREEMENT GABOLEH PUNYA 2 CUST
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  '1 AGREEMENT GABOLEH PUNYA 2 CUST' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO' AS [TABLE] ,
                AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(AAM.CUST_NO) AS SOME_COUNT, AAM.AGRMNT_NO 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING AAM WITH(NOLOCK)
                   GROUP BY AAM.AGRMNT_NO
                   HAVING COUNT(AAM.CUST_NO) > 1
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== 1 AGREENENT GABISA DI 2 OFFICE
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  '1 AGREENENT GABISA DI 2 OFFICE' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO' AS [TABLE] ,
                AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.AGRMNT_NO AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(AAM.OFFICE_CODE) AS SOME_COUNT, AAM.AGRMNT_NO 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING AAM WITH(NOLOCK)
                   GROUP BY AAM.AGRMNT_NO
                   HAVING COUNT(AAM.OFFICE_CODE) > 1
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== 1 ASSET GABOLEH MULTI AGREEMENT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  '1 ASSET GABOLEH MULTI AGREEMENT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(AAM.AGRMNT_NO) AS SOME_COUNT, AAM.ASSET_ID 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING AAM WITH(NOLOCK)
                   GROUP BY AAM.ASSET_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(AAM.AGRMNT_NO) > 1
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCRUED DT & ACCRUED AMT, START DT, END DT, RECOGNIZE DAYS HARUS ADA ISI
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ACCRUED DT & ACCRUED AMT, START DT, END DT, RECOGNIZE DAYS HARUS ADA ISI' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT A.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE A.ACCRUED_DT IS NULL OR A.ACCRUED_AMT IS NULL OR A.START_PERIOD IS NULL OR A.END_PERIOD IS NULL OR A.RECOGNIZE_DAYS IS NULL
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== CURR RATE GABOLE 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'CURR RATE GABOLE 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT A.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE CURR_RATE_AMT <= 0
                   
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL ACRRUED AMT DI D HARUS SAMA DENGAN ACCRUED AMT DI H
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL ACRRUED AMT DI D HARUS SAMA DENGAN ACCRUED AMT DI H' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN (
                     SELECT SUM(D.ACCRUED_AMT) AS SUM_D, D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                     FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL D WITH(NOLOCK)
                     GROUP BY D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                     ) AS D ON D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID = H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   WHERE H.ACCRUED_AMT <> D.SUM_D
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_MASTER RM WITH(NOLOCK) ON H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE = RM.MASTER_CODE
                   WHERE RM.MASTER_CODE IS NULL
                   GROUP BY H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACCRUED ,ACCRUED PLAN , OS ACCRUED, MONTHLY ACCRUED GABOLEH 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ACCRUED ,ACCRUED PLAN , OS ACCRUED, MONTHLY ACCRUED GABOLEH 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE H.ACCRUED_AMT = 0 OR H.ACCRUED_PLAN_AMT = 0 OR H.OS_ACCRUED_PLAN_AMT = 0 OR H.MONTHLY_ACCRUED_AMT = 0
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== START DT, END DT, LENGTH GABOLEH KOSONG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'START DT, END DT, LENGTH GABOLEH KOSONG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE H.ACCRUED_START_DT IS NULL OR H.ACCRUED_END_DT IS NULL OR H.ACCRUED_LENGTH IS NULL
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== END DATE HARUS = START DT + LENGTH (MONTH)
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'END DATE HARUS = START DT + LENGTH (MONTH)' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK) 
                   WHERE CONVERT(DATE, H.ACCRUED_END_DT) <> CONVERT(DATE, DATEADD(MONTH, H.ACCRUED_LENGTH, H.ACCRUED_START_DT))
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST SEQ NO HARUS = SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI D
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST SEQ NO HARUS = SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI D' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL D WITH(NOLOCK) ON D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID = H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL D2 WITH(NOLOCK) ON D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID = H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID AND D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID > D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID
                   WHERE D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID IS NULL AND H.LAST_SEQ_NO <> D.SEQ_NO
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST ACCRUED DT HARUS = ACCRUED DT TERAKHIR DI D
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST ACCRUED DT HARUS = ACCRUED DT TERAKHIR DI D' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL D WITH(NOLOCK) ON D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID = H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL D2 WITH(NOLOCK) ON D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID = H.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL_ID AND D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID > D.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID
                   WHERE D2.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL_ID IS NULL AND H.LAST_ACCRUED_DT <> D.ACCRUED_DT
                ) AS AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_ASSET_AMRTZ_ITEM_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                AGRMNT_ASSET_AMRTZ_ITEM_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_MASTER RM WITH(NOLOCK) ON H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE = RM.MASTER_CODE
                   WHERE RM.MASTER_CODE IS NULL
                   GROUP BY H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                ) AS AGRMNT_ASSET_AMRTZ_ITEM_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'REF ITEM CODE CEK KE REF MASTER' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ITEM_SCHDL_H_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                AMRTZ_ITEM_SCHDL_H_OPL.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(1) AS SOME_COUNT, H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                   FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_H_OPL H WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_MASTER RM WITH(NOLOCK) ON H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE = RM.MASTER_CODE
                   WHERE RM.MASTER_CODE IS NULL
                   GROUP BY H.REF_AMRTZ_ITEM_CODE
                ) AS AMRTZ_ITEM_SCHDL_H_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET DOC CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI ASSET DOC LIST JOIN REF_ASSET_DOC
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET DOC CODE HARUS TERDAFTAR DI ASSET DOC LIST JOIN REF_ASSET_DOC' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC.ASSET_DOC_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT AD.ASSET_DOC_CODE FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DOC AD WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_ASSET_DOC RAD WITH(NOLOCK) ON RAD.ASSET_DOC_CODE = AD.ASSET_DOC_CODE
                   LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST ADL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ADL.REF_ASSET_DOC_ID = RAD.REF_ASSET_DOC_ID
                   WHERE RAD.REF_ASSET_DOC_ID IS NULL AND ADL.ASSET_DOC_LIST_ID IS NULL
                ) AS ASSET_DOC
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET PRICE AMT , TOTAL ASSET PRICE AMT > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET PRICE AMT , TOTAL ASSET PRICE AMT > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT A.ASSET_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET A WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE A.ASSET_PRICE_AMT <= 0 OR A.TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT <= 0
                ) AS ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET STAT CODE HARUS ACT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET STAT CODE HARUS ACT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET.ASSET_STAT_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET.ASSET_STAT_CODE AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_STAT_CODE 
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE ASSET_STAT_CODE <> 'ACT' GROUP BY ASSET_STAT_CODE
                ) AS ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== PHYSICAL STAT = ONP KALAU ADA DATA DI AGRMNT ASSET MAPPING
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'PHYSICAL STAT = ONP KALAU ADA DATA DI AGRMNT ASSET MAPPING' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING_ID) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING ON AGRMNT_ASSET_MAPPING.ASSET_ID = ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   WHERE ASSET_STAT_CODE <> 'ONP'
                   GROUP BY ASSET.ASSET_ID
                ) AS ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== DLVRY ADDRESS + EXTRA HARUS DIISI KALAU INVENTORY STAT = PROD
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DLVRY ADDRESS + EXTRA HARUS DIISI KALAU INVENTORY STAT = PROD' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE INVENTORY_STAT_CODE = 'PROD' AND (DLVRY_ADDR IS NULL OR DLVRY_AREA_CODE_1 IS NULL OR DLVRY_AREA_CODE_2 IS NULL OR DLVRY_AREA_CODE_3 IS NULL OR DLVRY_AREA_CODE_4 IS NULL OR DLVRY_CITY IS NULL OR DLVRY_ZIPCODE IS NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET RECEIVE DT, ACTIVATION DT HARUS ADA
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET RECEIVE DT, ACTIVATION DT HARUS ADA' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE ASSET_RECEIVE_DT IS NULL OR ASSET_ACTIVATION_DT IS NULL
                ) AS ASSET_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ACTIVATION DT GABOLEH < RECEIVE DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ACTIVATION DT GABOLEH < RECEIVE DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE ASSET_ACTIVATION_DT < ASSET_RECEIVE_DT
                ) AS ASSET_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== BASE TAX, VAT AMT , ADDITIONAL FEE AMT, RESIDUAL VALUE PRCNT , RESIDUAL VALUE AMT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'BASE TAX, VAT AMT , ADDITIONAL FEE AMT, RESIDUAL VALUE PRCNT , RESIDUAL VALUE AMT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE BASE_TAX_AMT <= 0 OR VAT_AMT <= 0 OR ADDITIONAL_FEE_AMT <= 0 OR RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <= 0 OR RESIDUAL_VALUE_PRCNT <= 0
                ) AS ASSET_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL ASSET PRICE * RESIDUAL VALUE PRCNT HARUS = RESIDUAL VALUE AMT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL ASSET PRICE * RESIDUAL VALUE PRCNT HARUS = RESIDUAL VALUE AMT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET.ASSET_ID = ASSET_OPL.ASSET_ID
                   WHERE RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <> ( TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT * RESIDUAL_VALUE_PRCNT  / 100 )
                ) AS ASSET_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== MONTHLY , DAILY, OS , TOTAL, RESIDUAL HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'MONTHLY , DAILY, OS , TOTAL, RESIDUAL HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE MONTHLY_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR DAILY_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR OS_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT <= 0 OR RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <= 0
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA MR DEPRE STOP SRC CODE, HARUS ADA DEPRE STOP DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA MR DEPRE STOP SRC CODE, HARUS ADA DEPRE STOP DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE MR_DEPRE_STOP_SRC_CODE IS NOT NULL AND DEPRE_STOP_DT IS NULL
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== START, END GABOLEH KOSONG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'START, END GABOLEH KOSONG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_START_DT IS NULL OR DEPRE_END_DT IS NULL
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== START DT + LENGTH HARUS = END DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'START DT + LENGTH HARUS = END DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DATEADD(MONTH, DEPRE_LENGTH, DEPRE_START_DT) <> DEPRE_END_DT
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== DEPRE LENGTH GA BOLEH 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DEPRE LENGTH GA BOLEH 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_LENGTH <= 0
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST SEQ NO HARUS AMBIL SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST SEQ NO HARUS AMBIL SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT MAX(SEQ_NO) AS LAST_SEQ_NO, ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.LAST_SEQ_NO <> X.LAST_SEQ_NO
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST DEPRE DT HARUS AMBIL DEPRE DT TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST DEPRE DT HARUS AMBIL DEPRE DT TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT MAX(DEPRE_DT) AS LAST_DEPRE_DT, ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   WHERE AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.LAST_DEPRE_DT <> X.LAST_DEPRE_DT
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== NILAI RESIDUAL VALUE HARUS SAMA DENGAN RESIDUAL VALUE DI ASSET OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'NILAI RESIDUAL VALUE HARUS SAMA DENGAN RESIDUAL VALUE DI ASSET OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET ON ASSET.ASSET_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_ID
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL ON ASSET_OPL.ASSET_ID = ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <> ASSET_OPL.RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA IN AMT, EITHER ASSET ID ATAU ACCESSORY ID HARUS KEISI DAN SEQ NO NY NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA IN AMT, EITHER ASSET ID ATAU ACCESSORY ID HARUS KEISI DAN SEQ NO NY NULL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE IN_AMT IS NOT NULL AND ((ASSET_ID IS NULL AND ACCESSORY_ID IS NULL) AND SEQ_NO IS NOT NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA DEPRE AMT, ASSET ID & ACCESSORY ID HARUS NULL DAN HARUS ADA SEQ NO
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA DEPRE AMT, ASSET ID & ACCESSORY ID HARUS NULL DAN HARUS ADA SEQ NO' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_AMT IS NOT NULL AND ((ASSET_ID IS NOT NULL OR ACCESSORY_ID IS NOT NULL) AND SEQ_NO IS NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET DEPRE HARUS PUNYA DATA ASSET DEPRE TRX OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET DEPRE HARUS PUNYA DATA ASSET DEPRE TRX OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID) < 1
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SUM DEPRE AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN TOTAL ASSET PRICE - RESIDUAL - OS DEPRE AMT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SUM DEPRE AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN TOTAL ASSET PRICE - RESIDUAL - OS DEPRE AMT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) 
                   JOIN ( SELECT SUM(DEPRE_AMT) AS SUM_DEPRE_AMT, ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID ) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_OPL_ID
                   WHERE X.SUM_DEPRE_AMT <> TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT - RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT - OS_DEPRE_AMT
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== DATA HARUS ADA DI ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL & AMOUNT NYA HARUS SAMA (KEY : ASSET ID, DEPRE DT = TRANSACTION DT, PNL_TYPE = DEPRE) 
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DATA HARUS ADA DI ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL & AMOUNT NYA HARUS SAMA (KEY : ASSET ID, DEPRE DT = TRANSACTION DT, PNL_TYPE = DEPRE) ' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL.ASSET_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_ID AND AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.DEPRE_DT = AMS.dbo.ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL.TRANSACTION_DT AND MR_ASSET_PNL_TRX_TYPE_CODE = 'ASS_DEPRE_EXPENSE'
                   WHERE ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL_ID IS NULL OR (DEPRE_AMT <> EXPENSE_AMT)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== MONTHLY , DAILY, OS , TOTAL, RESIDUAL HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'MONTHLY , DAILY, OS , TOTAL, RESIDUAL HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE MONTHLY_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR DAILY_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR OS_DEPRE_AMT <= 0 OR TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT <= 0 OR RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <= 0
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA MR DEPRE STOP SRC CODE, HARUS ADA DEPRE STOP DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA MR DEPRE STOP SRC CODE, HARUS ADA DEPRE STOP DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE MR_DEPRE_STOP_SRC_CODE IS NOT NULL AND DEPRE_STOP_DT IS NULL
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== START, END GABOLEH KOSONG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'START, END GABOLEH KOSONG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_START_DT IS NULL OR DEPRE_END_DT IS NULL
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== START DT + LENGTH HARUS = END DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'START DT + LENGTH HARUS = END DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_END_DT <> DATEADD(MONTH, DEPRE_LENGTH,DEPRE_START_DT)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== DEPRE LENGTH GA BOLEH 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DEPRE LENGTH GA BOLEH 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_LENGTH <= 0
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST SEQ NO HARUS AMBIL SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST SEQ NO HARUS AMBIL SEQ NO TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT MAX(SEQ_NO) AS LAST_SEQ_NO, ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.LAST_SEQ_NO <> X.LAST_SEQ_NO
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== LAST DEPRE DT HARUS AMBIL DEPRE DT TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'LAST DEPRE DT HARUS AMBIL DEPRE DT TERAKHIR DI ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT MAX(DEPRE_DT) AS LAST_DEPRE_FISCAL_DT, ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   WHERE AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.LAST_DEPRE_DT <> X.LAST_DEPRE_FISCAL_DT
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== NILAI RESIDUAL VALUE HARUS SAMA DENGAN RESIDUAL VALUE DI ASSET OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'NILAI RESIDUAL VALUE HARUS SAMA DENGAN RESIDUAL VALUE DI ASSET OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL ON ASSET_OPL.ASSET_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_ID
                   WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT <> ASSET_OPL.RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA IN AMT, EITHER ASSET ID ATAU ACCESSORY ID HARUS KEISI DAN SEQ NO NY NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA IN AMT, EITHER ASSET ID ATAU ACCESSORY ID HARUS KEISI DAN SEQ NO NY NULL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE IN_AMT IS NOT NULL AND ((ASSET_ID IS NULL AND ACCESSORY_ID IS NULL) AND SEQ_NO IS NOT NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA DEPRE AMT, ASSET ID & ACCESSORY ID HARUS NULL DAN HARUS ADA SEQ NO
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA DEPRE AMT, ASSET ID & ACCESSORY ID HARUS NULL DAN HARUS ADA SEQ NO' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE DEPRE_AMT IS NOT NULL AND ((ASSET_ID IS NOT NULL OR ACCESSORY_ID IS NOT NULL) AND SEQ_NO IS NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== ASSET DEPRE HARUS PUNYA DATA ASSET DEPRE TRX OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'ASSET DEPRE HARUS PUNYA DATA ASSET DEPRE TRX OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT COUNT(ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID) < 1
                   
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SUM DEPRE AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN TOTAL ASSET PRICE - RESIDUAL - OS DEPRE AMT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SUM DEPRE AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN TOTAL ASSET PRICE - RESIDUAL - OS DEPRE AMT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) 
                   JOIN ( SELECT SUM(DEPRE_AMT) AS SUM_DEPRE_AMT, ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID ) X ON X.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID = ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL_ID
                   WHERE X.SUM_DEPRE_AMT <> TOTAL_ASSET_PRICE_AMT - RESIDUAL_VALUE_AMT - OS_DEPRE_AMT
                ) AS ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SETIAP ASSET HARUS PUNYA DATA LAST IN OUT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SETIAP ASSET HARUS PUNYA DATA LAST IN OUT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT_ID) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT ON ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT.ASSET_ID = ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   GROUP BY ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT_ID) < 1
                ) AS ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA NO, DATE NYA GABOLEH KOSONG (FIRST ASSET IN, LAST ASSET IN, LAST ASSET OUT, LAST ASSET DELIVERY)
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA NO, DATE NYA GABOLEH KOSONG (FIRST ASSET IN, LAST ASSET IN, LAST ASSET OUT, LAST ASSET DELIVERY)' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT.ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT.ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   
                   
                   
                   SELECT ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT
                   WHERE (FIRST_ASSET_IN_NO IS NOT NULL AND FIRST_ASSET_IN_DT IS NULL) OR (LAST_ASSET_IN_NO IS NOT NULL AND LAST_ASSET_IN_DT IS NULL) OR (LAST_ASSET_DLVRY_NO IS NOT NULL AND LAST_ASSET_DLVRY_DT IS NULL) OR (LAST_ASSET_OUT_NO IS NOT NULL AND LAST_ASSET_OUT_DT IS NULL)
                ) AS ASSET_LAST_IN_OUT
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== INCOME AMT & EXPENSE AMT GABISA DUA DUA NY 0, HARUS SALAH SATU, GA BOLEH JUGA DUA DUA NYA ADA ISI
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INCOME AMT & EXPENSE AMT GABISA DUA DUA NY 0, HARUS SALAH SATU, GA BOLEH JUGA DUA DUA NYA ADA ISI' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL.ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL.ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE (INCOME_AMT = 0 AND EXPENSE_AMT = 0) OR (INCOME_AMT > 0 AND EXPENSE_AMT > 0)
                ) AS ASSET_PROFIT_LOSS_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TIAP ASSET HARUS PUNYA ASSET REGISTRATION
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TIAP ASSET HARUS PUNYA ASSET REGISTRATION' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET.ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET.ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT COUNT(ASSET_REGISTRATION_ID) AS SOME_COUNT, ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_REGISTRATION ON ASSET_REGISTRATION.ASSET_ID = ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   GROUP BY ASSET.ASSET_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(ASSET_REGISTRATION_ID) < 1
                ) AS ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== INS_LENGTH HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INS_LENGTH HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE INS_LENGTH <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== CVG_AMT HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'CVG_AMT HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE CVG_AMT <= 0
                   
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA SPPA NO HARUS ADA SPPA DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA SPPA NO HARUS ADA SPPA DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE SPPA_NO IS NOT NULL AND SPPA_DT IS NULL
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SPPA NO & SPPA DATE HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SPPA NO & SPPA DATE HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.INS_SPPA_POLICY WITH(NOLOCK) ON INS_SPPA_POLICY.SPPA_NO = INS_ASSET.SPPA_NO AND INS_SPPA_POLICY.SPPA_DT = INS_ASSET.SPPA_DT
                   WHERE INS_SPPA_POLICY_ID IS NULL
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA POLICY NO HARUS ADA POLICY RCV DT
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA POLICY NO HARUS ADA POLICY RCV DT' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE POLICY_NO IS NOT NULL AND POLICY_RCV_DT IS NULL
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== POLICY NO & POLICY RCV DATE HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'POLICY NO & POLICY RCV DATE HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.INS_SPPA_POLICY WITH(NOLOCK) ON INS_SPPA_POLICY.POLICY_NO = INS_ASSET.POLICY_NO AND INS_SPPA_POLICY.POLICY_RCV_DT = INS_ASSET.POLICY_RCV_DT
                   WHERE INS_SPPA_POLICY_ID IS NULL
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU ADA ACTIVATION DT, DATA NY HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU ADA ACTIVATION DT, DATA NY HARUS ADA DI TABLE INS_SPPA_POLICY' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.INS_SPPA_POLICY WITH(NOLOCK) ON INS_SPPA_POLICY.INS_ASSET_ID = INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   WHERE INS_SPPA_POLICY.ACTIVATION_DT IS NOT NULL
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN (SELECT SUM(INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT) AS SUM_AMT, INS_ASSET_ID FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG GROUP BY INS_ASSET_ID) X ON X.INS_ASSET_ID = INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   WHERE TOTAL_INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT <> X.SUM_AMT
                   
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT SUM(INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT) SUM_AMT, INS_ASSET_ID FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG WITH(NOLOCK) JOIN AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG WITH(NOLOCK) ON INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID = INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID GROUP BY INS_ASSET_ID) X ON X.INS_ASSET_ID = INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   WHERE TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT <> X.SUM_AMT
                   
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL_INSCO_FEE_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_FEE_AMT DI INS_ASSET_FEE
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL_INSCO_FEE_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_FEE_AMT DI INS_ASSET_FEE' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN ( SELECT SUM(INSCO_FEE_AMT) AS SUM_FEE_AMT, INS_ASSET_ID FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_FEE WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY INS_ASSET_ID ) X ON X.INS_ASSET_ID = INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   WHERE TOTAL_INSCO_FEE_AMT <> X.SUM_FEE_AMT
                   
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== INS LENGTH HARUS SAMA DENGAN INS LENGTH DI INS_SPPA_POLICY
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INS LENGTH HARUS SAMA DENGAN INS LENGTH DI INS_SPPA_POLICY' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN AMS.dbo.INS_SPPA_POLICY ON INS_SPPA_POLICY.INS_ASSET_ID = INS_ASSET.INS_ASSET_ID
                   WHERE INS_ASSET.INS_LENGTH <> INS_SPPA_POLICY.INS_LENGTH
                   
                ) AS INS_ASSET
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SUM INSURED AMT > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SUM INSURED AMT > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE SUM_INSURED_AMT <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== INSCO MAIN PREMI AMT HARUS > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INSCO MAIN PREMI AMT HARUS > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE INSCO_MAIN_PREMI_AMT <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT HARUS SAMA DENGAN SUM INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT DI INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG WITH(NOLOCK)
                   JOIN (SELECT SUM(INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT) SUM_ADD_PREMI_AMT, INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG WITH(NOLOCK) GROUP BY INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID ) X ON X.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID = INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG.INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG_ID
                   WHERE TOTAL_INSCO_ADD_PREMI_AMT <> X.SUM_ADD_PREMI_AMT
                ) AS INS_ASSET_MAIN_CVG
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SUM INSURED AMT > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SUM INSURED AMT > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE SUM_INSURED_AMT <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== INSCO ADD PREMI AMT > 0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INSCO ADD PREMI AMT > 0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE

                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG.INS_ASSET_ADD_CVG_ID) AS VALUE

        --====================================== INSCO FEE AMT >  0
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'INSCO FEE AMT >  0' ,
                    [TABLE] ,

            From    (
