                   WHERE INSCO_FEE_AMT <= 0
                ) AS INS_ASSET_FEE
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SETIAP ASSET_OPL HARUS ADA DATA ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SETIAP ASSET_OPL HARUS ADA DATA ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL.ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL.ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT COUNT(ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL_ID) SOME_COUNT, ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID
                   FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                   LEFT JOIN AMS.dbo.ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID = ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID
                   GROUP BY ASSET_OPL.ASSET_OPL_ID
                   HAVING COUNT(ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL_ID) < 1
                ) AS ASSET_ENROLLMENT_OPL
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== SEMUA KOLOM ADDRESS PERLU DI SAMAIN DENGAN SEMUA KOLOM MALING ADDR DI AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO LMS
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'SEMUA KOLOM ADDRESS PERLU DI SAMAIN DENGAN SEMUA KOLOM MALING ADDR DI AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO LMS' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT_MAPPING.AGRMNT_MAPPING_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AGRMNT_MAPPING.AGRMNT_MAPPING_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT *
                   FROM CMS.dbo.AGRMNT_MAPPING
                   LEFT JOIN LMS.dbo.AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO ON AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_ADDR = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_ADDR 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_AREA_CODE_1 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_AREA_CODE_1 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_AREA_CODE_2 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_AREA_CODE_2 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_AREA_CODE_3 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_AREA_CODE_3 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_AREA_CODE_4 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_AREA_CODE_4 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_CITY = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_CITY 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_FAX = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_FAX 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_FAX_AREA = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_FAX_AREA 
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_PHN_1 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_PHN_1
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_PHN_2 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_PHN_2
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_PHN_EXT_1 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_PHN_EXT_1
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_PHN_EXT_2 = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_PHN_EXT_2
                   AND AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO.MAILING_ZIPCODE = AGRMNT_MAPPING.MAILING_ZIPCODE
                   WHERE AGRMNT_OTHER_INFO_ID IS NULL
                ) AS AGRMNT_MAPPING
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== KALAU CONTRACT STAT NY EXP, HARUS PUNYA EXP DATE, KALO BUKAN, EXP DATE NY NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'KALAU CONTRACT STAT NY EXP, HARUS PUNYA EXP DATE, KALO BUKAN, EXP DATE NY NULL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AGRMNT.AGRMNT_ID' AS [TABLE] ,
                CONVERT(NVARCHAR(1000), AGRMNT.AGRMNT_ID) AS VALUE
                FROM (
                    
                   SELECT AGRMNT_ID FROM LMS.dbo.AGRMNT WITH(NOLOCK)
                   WHERE ( CONTRACT_STAT_CODE = 'EXP' AND EXP_DT IS NULL) OR (CONTRACT_STAT_CODE <> 'EXP' AND EXP_DT IS NOT NULL)
                ) AS AGRMNT
                
        ) AS X

        --====================================== IS_ DIISI 0 ATAU 1, BUKAN Y ATAU N, TIDAK BOLEH NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'IS_ DIISI 0 ATAU 1, BUKAN Y ATAU N, TIDAK BOLEH NULL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                Select    'ASSET_ACCESSORY.IS_ACTIVE' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_ACCESSORY.IS_ACTIVE As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_ACCESSORY With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_ACTIVE Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_ACTIVE Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_ATTR.IS_EDITABLE_AFTER_GO_LIVE' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_ATTR.IS_EDITABLE_AFTER_GO_LIVE As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_ATTR With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_EDITABLE_AFTER_GO_LIVE Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_EDITABLE_AFTER_GO_LIVE Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_CATEGORY.IS_ACTIVE' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_CATEGORY.IS_ACTIVE As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_CATEGORY With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_ACTIVE Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_ACTIVE Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_MAIN_DOC' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_MAIN_DOC As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_MAIN_DOC Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_MAIN_DOC Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_VALUE_NEEDED' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_VALUE_NEEDED As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_VALUE_NEEDED Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_VALUE_NEEDED Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_PLEDGE' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_PLEDGE As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_PLEDGE Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_PLEDGE Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_BORROW' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_BORROW As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_BORROW Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_BORROW Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_MANDATORY_NEW' As [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_MANDATORY_NEW As VALUE
                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_MANDATORY_NEW Not In ( 1, 0 )
                Or IS_MANDATORY_NEW Is Null
                
                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_DOC_LIST.IS_MANDATORY_USED' As [TABLE] ,

                From      MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_DOC_LIST With ( NoLock )
                Where     IS_MANDATORY_USED Not In ( 1, 0 )

                UNION

                UNION

                Select    'ASSET_MASTER.IS_FINAL' As [TABLE] ,

                Or IS_ACTIVE Is Null

        --====================================== DATA TIDAK DITEMUKAN DI TABEL JOIN
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DATA TIDAK DITEMUKAN DI TABEL JOIN' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE  COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AS VALUE
                FROM MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.CUST_OTHER_INFO WITH(NOLOCK)
                LEFT JOIN MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP WITH(NOLOCK) ON LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE = CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE
                WHERE LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_DEBT_GRP_CODE
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE  COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AS VALUE
                FROM MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.CUST_OTHER_INFO WITH(NOLOCK)
                LEFT JOIN MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL WITH(NOLOCK) ON LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE = CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE
                WHERE LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY CUST_OTHER_INFO.LBPPMS_BIZ_SCL_CODE
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'CUST_PERSONAL.WNA_COUNTRY_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                CUST_PERSONAL.WNA_COUNTRY_CODE  COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AS VALUE
                FROM MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.CUST_PERSONAL WITH(NOLOCK)
                LEFT JOIN MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.REF_COUNTRY WITH(NOLOCK) ON REF_COUNTRY.COUNTRY_CODE = CUST_PERSONAL.WNA_COUNTRY_CODE
                WHERE REF_COUNTRY.COUNTRY_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY CUST_PERSONAL.WNA_COUNTRY_CODE
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'CUST_PERSONAL_EMERGENCY_CONTACT.NATIONALITY_COUNTRY_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                CUST_PERSONAL_EMERGENCY_CONTACT.NATIONALITY_COUNTRY_CODE  COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AS VALUE
                FROM MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.CUST_PERSONAL_EMERGENCY_CONTACT WITH(NOLOCK)
                LEFT JOIN MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.REF_COUNTRY WITH(NOLOCK) ON REF_COUNTRY.COUNTRY_CODE = CUST_PERSONAL_EMERGENCY_CONTACT.NATIONALITY_COUNTRY_CODE

                LEFT JOIN MIGRATION_OPL.dbo.ASSET_CATEGORY WITH(NOLOCK) ON ASSET_CATEGORY.ASSET_CATEGORY_CODE = VENDOR_INSCO_BRANCH_SUM_INS.INS_ASSET_CATEGORY_CODE
                WHERE ASSET_CATEGORY.ASSET_CATEGORY_CODE IS NULL

                WHERE ASSET_MASTER.FULL_ASSET_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY REF_MARKET_PRICE_X.FULL_ASSET_CODE
                
                UNION

                WHERE ASSET.ASSET_ID IS NULL
                GROUP BY ASSET_OPL.ASSET_ID
                
        ) AS X
        --====================================== DATA TIDAK BOLEH NULL
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DATA TIDAK BOLEH NULL' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'ASSET.MANUFACTURING_YEAR' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET.ASSET_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET.MANUFACTURING_YEAR IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET.COLOR' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET.ASSET_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET.COLOR IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET.TAX_CITY_ISSUER' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET.ASSET_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET.TAX_CITY_ISSUER IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET.TAX_ISSUE_DT' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET.ASSET_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET.TAX_ISSUE_DT IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.DEPRE_DT' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_TRX_OPL.DEPRE_DT IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.DEPRE_DT' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET_DEPRE_FISCAL_TRX_OPL.DEPRE_DT IS NULL
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET_REGISTRATION.OWNER_ID_NO' AS [TABLE] ,
                ASSET_REGISTRATION.ASSET_REGISTRATION_ID AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.ASSET_REGISTRATION WITH(NOLOCK)
                WHERE ASSET_REGISTRATION.OWNER_ID_NO IS NULL
                
                UNION

              [TABLE] ,

        --====================================== DATA STATUS BELUM TERDAFTAR
    
        Insert  Into INTEGRITY_CHECK
            ( ISSUE ,
              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )
            Select  'DATA STATUS BELUM TERDAFTAR' ,
                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE
            From    (
        
                SELECT 'AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.RECOGNIZE_STAT_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,
                AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL.RECOGNIZE_STAT_CODE COLLATE Latin1_General_CI_AI AS VALUE
                FROM AMS.dbo.AMRTZ_ASSET_ITEM_D_OPL WITH(NOLOCK)
                LEFT JOIN FOUNDATION.dbo.REF_STATUS WITH(NOLOCK) ON REF_STATUS.REF_STATUS_CODE = RECOGNIZE_STAT_CODE AND REF_STATUS.STATUS_GRP_CODE = 'RECOGNIZE_STAT'
                WHERE REF_STATUS_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY RECOGNIZE_STAT_CODE
                
                UNION

                SELECT 'ASSET_DOC.DOC_STAT_CODE' AS [TABLE] ,

                    [TABLE] ,

              [TABLE] ,
              VALUE
            )

                    [TABLE] ,
                    VALUE

                FROM LMS.dbo.AGRMNT WITH(NOLOCK)

                WHERE MASTER_CODE IS NULL
                GROUP BY LC_CALC_METHOD
